<div id="review_159906999" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/159906999" />
    <a title=" Danielle The Book Huntress (Back to the Books)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books"><img alt=" Danielle The Book Huntress (Back to the Books)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1403239075p2/1570669.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/159906999?book_show_action=true">Apr 09, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title=" Danielle The Book Huntress (Back to the Books)" class="user" itemprop="url" name=" Danielle The Book Huntress (Back to the Books)" href="/user/show/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books"> Danielle The Book Huntress (Back to the Books)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">PNR romance readers</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=hero-to-die-for">hero-to-die-for</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=mountain-man-or-woman">mountain-man-or-woman</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=antihero">antihero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=possessive-and-or-jealous-hero">possessive-and-or-jealous-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=hero-i-want-to-lick">hero-i-want-to-lick</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=immortality">immortality</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=favorite-or-autobuy-author">favorite-or-autobuy-author</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=cold-or-forbidding-hero">cold-or-forbidding-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=royalty">royalty</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=revenge">revenge</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer159906999" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12560439663114841938"><b>Listened to audiobook between 1/2019 and 3/2019. Robert Petkoff is an excellent audiobook narrator. He's great at accents and equally skilled at portraying male and female characters. He made each personality distinctive. This is still one of my all time favorites in the series.<br/><br/>Previous Review Below</b>-----------<br/><br/><br/>I loved this book! This was worth waiting for, even though it was a long wait for it to come out in paperback. I can say that the hours spent reading it were truly enjoyable. It's true that</span>
  <span id="freeText12560439663114841938" style="display:none"><b>Listened to audiobook between 1/2019 and 3/2019. Robert Petkoff is an excellent audiobook narrator. He's great at accents and equally skilled at portraying male and female characters. He made each personality distinctive. This is still one of my all time favorites in the series.<br /><br />Previous Review Below</b>-----------<br /><br /><br />I loved this book! This was worth waiting for, even though it was a long wait for it to come out in paperback. I can say that the hours spent reading it were truly enjoyable. It's true that I am a huge fan of this series, but it never gets old for me. I do believe this is one of the best paranormal series out there, hands down! It has a lot of sex, so I wouldn't recommend it to a fantasy fan who doesn't like sex, but I feel that the world-building stands up to muster for a fantasy novel as well. I think that this story keeps expanding in ways that intrigue and fascinate me. I am happily surprised at all the twists and turns Cole gives this storyline.<br /><br />Lothaire totally lived up to his potential. He is all that and more. I think that Cole did a great job of giving this character a romance without compromising who he was. Lothaire will always be a bad guy. He is just a bad guy who sometimes does the right thing. Kind of different and it worked for me! I have a <s>sick fascination</s> weakness for villainous/antiheroic types, and Lothaire is the top of the list!<br /><br /><b>Things I loved about Lothaire</b><br />*Lothaire stays true to his character. He doesn't become a Stepford Hero just because he finds his true love. He is always going to be Lothaire, just Lothaire in love.<br />*He cracks me up. I know he's not trying to be funny. He's just being him, but his way of twisting his words to get around his physiological demand to be truthful, and his sheer arrogance, results in some laugh out loud, snarkalicious comments. I can imagine Ms. Cole cracked herself and her editor up reading as she wrote it. I know she cracked me up.<br />*I love a wickedly intelligent guy. My Achilles' heel. Lothaire is such a calculating dude. Always working all the angles. It was interesting to see how others reacted to him. Many hated him, some were scared witless by him, and some admired him (in a "I hate him" kind of way). No one was 'meh' about him.<br />*Lothaire actually wants to be faithful to his Bride. <br /><br /><b>Things I loved about Elizabeth</b><br />*She's very tough considering all that she went through. (Shudders) I can't imagine having that awful thing taking over my body committing those horrible acts with it. And then, where she spent five years! That was so dark!<br />*She's so down to earth. I love a down to earth heroine. She's very proud of her humble root, loves her family, and is unshakably loyal.<br />*She holds her own with Lothaire. Maybe she doesn't have thousands of years of experience or his incredible, immortal strength, but she has a snarky tongue, plenty of intelligence, and a big heart.<br /><br /><b>Things I loved about this book</b><br />*Kresley Cole never tries to sell this as a normal people/functional romance. From the beginning, it's clear that this is not for the faint of heart. Lothaire is not a kind, loving, good-hearted boy next door. He is the Enemy of Old. Ellie is not the normal girl next door with a sweet, happy existence. Her life was tough since she was young, and it turns into a living hell when she's eighteen, and things just get worse. Despite that, I found it to be a sigh-worthy romance. I don't want a Lothaire of my own, but I sure did like reading about his romance with Ellie!<br />*Lothaire has met his match in Ellie. Although he tried to walk all over her, he finds out the hard way that's not going to fly. Ellie proves to be a dangerous woman in her own right. If you have read this, you'll find out.<br />*I didn't find this to be predictable. I had my ideas about how things would work out, but I was wrong! In fact, I was thrown a loop a time or two. I love how Cole turns all the endgame goals of Lothaire on their heads.<br />*Freaking hilarious. Despite the very dark beginning and dark subject matter, there is much to enjoy and laugh about this book.<br />*Smoking hot love scenes. I mean, wow! (thinks about the scenes and wipes forehead)<br />*This world is endlessly fascinating and entertaining. All the different characters and how their immortal lives intersect. I like seeing the plots come together and overlap. With each book, I just want more.<br /><br />Over five hundred pages of fantastic goodness. And when it ended, I was sad. I want to read it over again, but no time. Good thing I am planning on an Immortals After Dark series reread early next year!<br /><br />Thumbs Way Up!!! This is a Goodread For Sure!</span>
  <a data-text-id="12560439663114841938" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/210123-d-g?shelf=steamy">steamy</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer931007305" class="readable"

  <span id="freeText15003166622019995911" style="display:none"><b>Lothaire's review in two songs. <br /><br />Part I - THE CHARACTER (Lothaire)</b><br />Sing to the music of <a href="https://youtu.be/wyx6JDQCslE?t=57s" rel="nofollow noopener">Sexy and I know it</a> by LMFAO.<br /><br />♪♫♬<br /><i>I'm evil and I love it<br />I'm evil and I love it<br /><br />When I'm at Val Hall, the Valkyries want to kill me all<br />But they can't beat me, they're not even on my league, (what?)<br />I'm the Enemy of Old, I've betrayed half the Lore<br />No matter who they are, I make them nervous <br />No Lykae, no Demon, no Lorian, don't compare us (watch)<br /><br />Ah...Just look at that body<br />Ah...Just look at that face<br />Ah...Just look at that brain<br />I'm so bad<br /><br />Ah...Just look at that body<br />Ah...Just look at that face<br />Ah...Just look at that brain<br />I'm so mad<br /><br />When I walk in the Lore, this is what I see<br />Everybody stops and they want to kill me<br />I'm the Enemy of Old and they're afraid to fight me, fight me, fight me<br /><br />I'm evil and I love it<br />I'm evil and I love it</i><br />♪♫♬<br /><br /><b>Part II - THE RELATIONSHIP</b><br />Sing to the music of <a href="https://youtu.be/E8gmARGvPlI?t=15s" rel="nofollow noopener">Last Christmas</a> by Wham!<br /><br />♪♫♬<br /><i>At Vall Hall I gave you my heart<br />But the very next day you flipped me the bird<br />(You flipped me the bird)<br />Indeed!     <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_154438218" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/154438218" />
    <a title="Annie (Under the Covers Book Blog)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog"><img alt="Annie (Under the Covers Book Blog)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1352609417p2/2489554.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/154438218?book_show_action=true">Mar 14, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Annie (Under the Covers Book Blog)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Annie (Under the Covers Book Blog)" href="/user/show/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog">Annie (Under the Covers Book Blog)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">IAD fans, PNR fans</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=author-kresley-cole">author-kresley-cole</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=books-i-go-rabid-over">books-i-go-rabid-over</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=books-i-own">books-i-own</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=covers-to-covet">covers-to-covet</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=signed-by-author">signed-by-author</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=drinks-on-me">drinks-on-me</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=king-of-the-harem">king-of-the-harem</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=vampires">vampires</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=my-hottie-harem">my-hottie-harem</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer154438218" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9978779165441646569"><b>Posted on <a href='http://underthecoversbookblog.blogspot.com/2012/01/review-giveaway-lothaire-by-kresley.html' rel='nofollow noopener'></a> Under the Covers</b><br/><br/>Lothaire the Enemy of Old possess an insatiable need for revenge against the Horde. After being cast out along with his Dacian mother by his father and King of the Horde vampires, Stefanovich, Lothaire vows to his mother that he will slay his father and become king one day. His plans include uniting the Dacian and Horde kingdoms together. This is his endgame, his raison d’etre. <br/><br/><br/>That is until Elizabeth Pierce stumbles upon his life. Ellie, as she is most often called in</span>
  <span id="freeText9978779165441646569" style="display:none"><b>Posted on <a href="http://underthecoversbookblog.blogspot.com/2012/01/review-giveaway-lothaire-by-kresley.html" rel="nofollow noopener"></a> Under the Covers</b><br /><br />Lothaire the Enemy of Old possess an insatiable need for revenge against the Horde. After being cast out along with his Dacian mother by his father and King of the Horde vampires, Stefanovich, Lothaire vows to his mother that he will slay his father and become king one day. His plans include uniting the Dacian and Horde kingdoms together. This is his endgame, his raison d’etre. <br /><br /><br />That is until Elizabeth Pierce stumbles upon his life. Ellie, as she is most often called in this book could not be more different than Lothaire. He, dark, cunning and lethal. She, a spit-fire, loyal and loving. Though Ellie is a mere mortal, her body is inhabited by a death goddess named Saroya. Once powerful, Saroya is now condemned to live within mortal bodies. She lives to draw blood and deal death, which is why whenever Saroya surfaces and takes control of her body, Ellie wakes up to find herself in a bloodbath. <br /><br /><br /><br />When Lothaire meets Saroya/Ellie, he becomes blooded. His heart begins to beat after centuries of remaining still. His lungs fill with breath once again. And ... other things begin to stir to life. Naturally, Lothaire, the maddened and most feared vampire in the Lore believes that Saroya is his Bride, not the hillbilly mountain girl. But in order for him to claim his Bride, Lothaire must dispose of Ellie’s soul from the body and make Saroya immortal, a vampire like him. <br /><br /><br /><br />To do this, he must obtain a ring. This ring holds his one chance to keep his Bride, except locating it is his greatest problem. <br /><br /><br /><br />In the meantime, Lothaire saves Ellie from jail where she is being held and almost killed. Saving her from death row doesn’t get any points for him because Ellie actually wants to die. To die would mean there would be no more innocent deaths on her head, and Ellie wants nothing more than peace. <br /><br /><br /><br />Together, Ellie and Lothaire combust. One who is used to getting his way all the time, Lothaire isn’t used to the way Ellie refuses him. There were times when I wanted to slap him for hurting Ellie, but as you read this book, you learn that Lothaire never had any relationships before this. He has no friends, just a ledger with names scrawled on the pages that record the debts that must be paid to him. His madness is his only company, forever torturing him, allowing him no reprieve. <br /><br /><br /><br />Cole stays true to Lothaire’s character. She doesn’t suddenly make him a “good guy” now that he is the hero of his own book. Called the Enemy of Old, Lothaire has created that name for himself. He remains ruthless and cunning, sometimes to the point where his actions are unforgiveable. <br /><br /><br /><br />Though a mere mortal, Ellie sinks his claws into Lothaire. It was enjoyable to read his emotions – confusion, anger, distrust. No one else throws Lothaire for a loop like Ellie does. Lothaire reacts to Ellie in a way no like other. It is only then that the question of Saroya being his true Bride arises: <br /><br /><br /><br /><i>“Are you certain she’s not your Bride?” <br />“Careful, Hag,” he warned her, seething that she would even consider Elizabeth for him. “Your past employers might have forgiven your impudence; I will not.” <br />“I never predicted your female would be Saroya.” <br />“In so many words, you did. ‘A great and fearless queen beloved by vampires, who will secure your throne for you,’” he said. “Ellie Ann, late of Appalachia, just isn’t going to inspire Hordely, vampirely love.” </i><br /><br />Though their times together may not be all hearts and goo-goo eyes, apart, Ellie and Lothaire wither. It is this conversation with Nix, everyone’s favourite cray cray soothsayer that became one of my favourite parts of this book: <br /><br /><br /><i>He scrubbed a hand over his face. “I didn’t feel old when I was with Elizabeth. I felt like a young vampire, just starting out with her. The world was ours for the taking.” <br />“I envy you that feeling.” <br />After several heartbeats, he admitted in a low voice, “I’d go back to the grave if it would force Elizabeth to love me.”</i> <br /><br />What I loved about this book is that Lothaire and Ellie choose to make their relationship work. Fate may play a big part in choosing a Bride, but Ellie has the ultimate say in all things. I loved watching Lothaire be brought to his knees by the woman he loves. <br /><br /><br />LOTHAIRE - just as the self-titled book entails - will demand your attention until you flip that last page! Just as addicting as the rest of the series, Cole is my new brand of crack. I’d do anything for that next hit!<br /><br />*Review copy provided by publisher</span>
  <a data-text-id="9978779165441646569" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_170771555" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/170771555" />
    <a title="Suzanne (Under the Covers Book blog)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3575839-suzanne-under-the-covers-book-blog"><img alt="Suzanne (Under the Covers Book blog)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1583236251p2/3575839.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/170771555?book_show_action=true">May 24, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Suzanne (Under the Covers Book blog)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Suzanne (Under the Covers Book blog)" href="/user/show/3575839-suzanne-under-the-covers-book-blog">Suzanne (Under the Covers Book blog)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Hardcover 9780857207975" href="/book/show/13112924-lothaire">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3575839-suzanne-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=lover-the-cover">lover-the-cover</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3575839-suzanne-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=paranormal-menagerie">paranormal-menagerie</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3575839-suzanne-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=va-va-voom-vampires">va-va-voom-vampires</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3575839-suzanne-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=mages-witches-magic-users">mages-witches-magic-users</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3575839-suzanne-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=author-kresley-cole">author-kresley-cole</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3575839-suzanne-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=shifters">shifters</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3575839-suzanne-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=genre-paranormal-romance">genre-paranormal-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3575839-suzanne-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=best-of-the-best-2012">best-of-the-best-2012</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer170771555" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10912767682845490145">I have a confession to make. I didn't think this book would live up to my expectations, secretly, I started reading this expecting it to disappoint me. How could it not? Lothaire the Enemy of Old has been in these books from the beginning, we have had 11 books building his character up, making us adore and worship him <i>despite</i> the fact that he is undeniably evil and insane and would happily murder all our other favourite characters. Yet still we long for a happy ending for him, Kresley Cole has u</span>
  <span id="freeText10912767682845490145" style="display:none">I have a confession to make. I didn't think this book would live up to my expectations, secretly, I started reading this expecting it to disappoint me. How could it not? Lothaire the Enemy of Old has been in these books from the beginning, we have had 11 books building his character up, making us adore and worship him <i>despite</i> the fact that he is undeniably evil and insane and would happily murder all our other favourite characters. Yet still we long for a happy ending for him, Kresley Cole has us on in her thrall!<br /><br />I figure if you have read this book, or are about to, then you don't really need a synopsis of what is happening, you know who Lothaire is and I don't want to give anything away that will ruin it for you. If you haven't started this series then you need to read: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/6388558.The_Warlord_Wants_Forever__Immortals_After_Dark___1_" title="The Warlord Wants Forever (Immortals After Dark, #1) by Kresley Cole" rel="nofollow noopener">The Warlord Wants Forever</a> or <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/14384.A_Hunger_Like_No_Other__Immortals_After_Dark___2_" title="A Hunger Like No Other (Immortals After Dark, #2) by Kresley Cole" rel="nofollow noopener">A Hunger Like No Other</a> first and work your way through this fabulous series. <br /><br />Another confession, showing my dire lack of faith in the almight Kresley Cole, is that I couldn't think of female that would match Lothaire, perhaps, apart from Nix, but yet again I was gladly proved incorrect, Elizabeth Peirce (Ellie to her friends) was a great fit. Good to his bad, sane to his insane, happy to his misery... you couldn't help but like her. As for Lothaire, there is so much more to him then being the insane bad guy, his Endgame comes into focus and we begin to see a different side to him, still evil ofcourse, but I can't seem to help loving the bad boys. And his arrogance, how can something so damn annoying if it were real, be so damn sexy?!<br /><br />Like all the other books in this series, this was sexy (spare knickers required), funny and full of unforgettable characters. One of the best things about Kresley Cole's books are that the heroines are just as good as the heroes, something I have found to be rare in romance, which only makes me feel a little guilty now that I have poached Lothaire to be in my harem!<br /><br />p.s. Don't worry Lachlain, you are still my favourite!<br /><br /><b>Quotes I Loved</b><br /><br /><i>"Yes, you. An ignorant mortal Kmart checkout girl." He took the sharpest knife from his place setting, absently turning it between his left thumb and forefinger.<br /><br />"Kmart? I should've been so lucky. Those jobs were hard to come by. I worked at my uncle's outfitter hop."<br /><br />"Then you're even worse. You're an outfitter checkout girl with aspirations for Kmart."</i><br /><br />*****<br /><br /><i>"Everything you've ever dreamed is real," Lothaire said. "Every creature thought to be myth. We call our world the Lore. And for the record, Mothman's a fuckwit."</i><br /><br />*****<br /><br /><i>"You are so maieve, it physically aggrieves me."</i><br /><br />*****<br /><br /><i>"First of all I'm not narcissitic." When she opened her lips to argue he said, "I know Narkissos of Thespiae- while we might share traits, i cam first so he's Lothairistic, not the other way round."</i><br /><br />*****<br /><br /><i>"And how is it that you could possibly pity me?"<br /><br />"I'm twenty-four years old. I've spent more then twenty percent of my life on death row. And I've still known more happiness in my short life than you have in your unending one."</i><br /><br />*****<br /><br /><i>Has anything really changed?" (Ellie)<br /><br />"I've learned I need to consult you in matters, lest you decapitate me."<br /><br />*****<br /><br />"What is this? Be like you were with me the oher times! When you melted for me."<br /><br />"That was before I fully understood what a nasty piece of work you are."<br /><br />"Because of a few shifter beheadings? Come on, Lizvetta, it's not as if I went round cock slapping gnomes."</i></span>
  <a data-text-id="10912767682845490145" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_154572726" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/154572726" />
    <a title="Zeek" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2478293-zeek"><img alt="Zeek" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1339154824p2/2478293.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/154572726?book_show_action=true">Mar 15, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Zeek" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Zeek" href="/user/show/2478293-zeek">Zeek</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2478293-zeek?shelf=favorite-author">favorite-author</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2478293-zeek?shelf=pnr-kitchen-sink">pnr-kitchen-sink</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2478293-zeek?shelf=alpha-hero">alpha-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2478293-zeek?shelf=favorite-heroine">favorite-heroine</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2478293-zeek?shelf=pnr">pnr</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2478293-zeek?shelf=shifters">shifters</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2478293-zeek?shelf=angels-gods-demons">angels-gods-demons</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2478293-zeek?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2478293-zeek?shelf=vamps">vamps</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2478293-zeek?shelf=witches">witches</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer154572726" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer402920044769607226">Sad to say this one was not a 5 star for me as many of her others in this series were. In fact, I vacillate between just thinking it was okay to liking it to really liking it because the parts I liked? I <i>really</i> liked!<br/><br/>Let me synop it a bit then give you my reasons why.<br/><br/>Lothaire, the ancient vampire known as The Enemy of Old, has an endgame...vengeance upon his paternity who so betrayed his mother a thousand yrs ago. He’ll use any piece on the chessboard his master of a mind can get his hands on to</span>
  <span id="freeText402920044769607226" style="display:none">Sad to say this one was not a 5 star for me as many of her others in this series were. In fact, I vacillate between just thinking it was okay to liking it to really liking it because the parts I liked? I <i>really</i> liked!<br /><br />Let me synop it a bit then give you my reasons why.<br /><br />Lothaire, the ancient vampire known as The Enemy of Old, has an endgame...vengeance upon his paternity who so betrayed his mother a thousand yrs ago. He’ll use any piece on the chessboard his master of a mind can get his hands on to achieve it- including the woman fated to be his “Bride”, his mate for immortal life whom can only make him stronger. One catch- his mate, a Goddess of death and destruction, is trapped inside the nubile body of hillbilly from the Appalachian mountains of America. <br /><br />The nubile young body, (a very much sentient Elizabeth Peirce), knows she’s possessed by something unutterably evil, she’s awoken too many times in the midst of too many broken bloody bodies strewn about to doubt that. But she’s determined to rid the world of this malicious creature- by destroying herself.<br /><br />But a wicked blond haired, red-eyed, devil wants otherwise- and he’s holding her captive till he can rid the world of <i>her</i> rather than the evil goddess, Saroya, (the being he thinks is his mate). <br /><br />But, as people have all her life, The Enemy of Old has underestimated this seeming backward girl from the poorest of the poor and when he finally realizes the truth, there’s a good possibility he’ll lose everything- even his much desired throne.<br /><br />Lothaire's story became a disappointment to me for reasons other than the characters- which is usually the biggest downfall for me when grading a book... If I don’t “get” the characters- you’ve lost me. But I will say something about Lothaire himself never fully grabbed me. I found him lacking in depth UNTIL we saw him through Thad’s eyes long after the middle of the book.<br /><br />For the most part, I felt the book plotted with a heavy hand, (“I’ve been betrayed all my life, gee I hope she doesn’t betray me.” hmmm wonder if she’ll betray him?) and was decidedly lacking in KC's trademark wit. In <i>fact</i>, she borrowed from Dreams of a Dark Warrior to bring in some humor over Lothaire, having Thadd recount some of Lothaire's funnier lines from <i>that</i> book. Don’t get me wrong there were some damn funny bits with the valkeries toward the end which made the last third of the book my favorite part of the book and the most memorable. Odd that it was when they were separated? I am a bit curious about their lives together after this book. For some reason its difficult to picture them in something as mundane as marital life with a pack of kiddoes. <br /><br />Another issue for me? The scene jumping. I had a difficult time figuring out why we were suddenly in another scene, and that happened more than once. It made me wonder if KC had written more to this story and then hacked it up later? Maybe. Probably. Whatever. It just didn’t feel right.<br /><br />Ultimately, I kept waiting to fully immerse myself in the story but ended up merely going along for the ride, which became my biggest disappointment. <br /><br />And I gotta say, they were indeed <i>perfect</i> for each other- even though his prejudice against her upbringing nearly ended it. She was empathetic, smart and determined and she didn’t back down- exactly what Bitter Bossypants needed. And I just LOVED watching him want her. The fact that he figured out she's way more attractive then the stupid bitch goddess inside her because she was <i>kind</i>, made me finally be okay with him. <br /><br /> Bonus: ‘Nix!- we get her full name, which we might have before but I couldn’t remember, and a little more insight into the burden she carries. She’s the biggest manipulator of them all and nobody knows how long she’s been playing at it- except for perhaps Lothaire, her once boon companion. <i>Now</i>-after seeing her here- I’m seriously curious as to who will mate her… and how this apocalypse is gonna play out. She’s gotta a lot of things to manipulate to make it work out fine for her pals- but I think she just may do it. ;)<br /><br />Finally- c’mon he’s a prince and heir to two thrones and she’s a modern day peasant, <i>and</i>, he ends up a sad sack without her-because she’s a fighter and he has no idea how wrong her is about her. And that in the end he will tear his heart out to have her in his arms. what romance reading gal doesn’t fall for a couple like that?? <br /><br />So, okay, yes I was disappointed- not because I anticipated Lothaire’s story so much, because honestly I didn’t, but because I anticipate <i>any</i> story from K. Cole. <br /><br />Still I’m giving it a grudging 3.5 stars-for all the reasons above... Lothaire and his downfall, Lizvetta- who <i>becomes</i> his means to an end- are worth the read!<br /><br />(and yes, I'm still very excited I bought the signed, limited edition copy of this story- because I still think this is the best Paranormal Romance series out there right now!!)</span>
  <a data-text-id="402920044769607226" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer11241600850431322151"><br/>I can't ... I mean I CAN NOT express the amount of love I feel for this series! I am talking BURSTING with FEELS! From appreciation for the author and her ability to deliver the most unique story-line/couple/conflict with each and every book to falling in love with anti-hero you have no business of falling in love with. From rooting for THE most kick ass female leads to laughing your butt off at all kinds of pop-culture references. From shedding a tear [or several] when your heart aches for thes</span>
  <span id="freeText11241600850431322151" style="display:none"><br />I can't ... I mean I CAN NOT express the amount of love I feel for this series! I am talking BURSTING with FEELS! From appreciation for the author and her ability to deliver the most unique story-line/couple/conflict with each and every book to falling in love with anti-hero you have no business of falling in love with. From rooting for THE most kick ass female leads to laughing your butt off at all kinds of pop-culture references. From shedding a tear [or several] when your heart aches for these characters who happen to be immortals but manage to provoke all kinds of human feels in a reader to fist pumping when said characters finally manage to arrive at their well deserved HEA. I can go on but one MUST experience the beauty of Kresley Cole's magical storytelling for themselves to fully 'get' what I am trying to say. This author has become my one-click author for a reason. At this point, I am convinced she can't write a bad book even if she tried. The way she tells a story is so natural that I find myself flipping pages at super [for me] speed and I am one of THE slowest readers on Earth! I am never bored &amp; always feel like I am <i>there</i>, in the midst of the action with some of the most fascinating characters I've ever had a pleasure of reading about. Absolute PERFECTION from start to finish. Every. Single Time. If you enjoyed fairy tales as a child and love letting your imagination run wild as an adult, this series is for you!<br /></span>

<div id="review_179779123" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/179779123" />
    <a title="When Funmi Met Romance" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5615242-when-funmi-met-romance"><img alt="When Funmi Met Romance" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1572219419p2/5615242.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/179779123?book_show_action=true">Jun 26, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="When Funmi Met Romance" class="user" itemprop="url" name="When Funmi Met Romance" href="/user/show/5615242-when-funmi-met-romance">When Funmi Met Romance</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">romance readers, paranormal romance lovers, EVERYONE</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5615242-when-funmi-met-romance?shelf=2012-reread">2012-reread</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5615242-when-funmi-met-romance?shelf=great-sex">great-sex</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5615242-when-funmi-met-romance?shelf=hero-royalty">hero-royalty</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5615242-when-funmi-met-romance?shelf=heroines-bad-past-suffering-abused">heroines-bad-past-suffering-abused</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5615242-when-funmi-met-romance?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5615242-when-funmi-met-romance?shelf=ptsd-suffering-scarred-heroes">ptsd-suffering-scarred-heroes</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5615242-when-funmi-met-romance?shelf=2012">2012</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5615242-when-funmi-met-romance?shelf=paranormal-romance">paranormal-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5615242-when-funmi-met-romance?shelf=not-released">not-released</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5615242-when-funmi-met-romance?shelf=strong-best-heroines">strong-best-heroines</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer179779123" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16135401283051110102"><b>Lothaire (Immortals after Dark, #12: 5 Star read that doesn't fail to deliver an amazing read</b><br/><br/><b>General Thoughts:</b> I love this series beyond reason. How is it that every freaking book manages to get better and better. I have no clue. Hopefully you are in the process of reading this book or reading the series because I can't help but feel like its one of the best ones out there. I never read paranormal romance until I stumbled across this series and it was the best stumble I've ever had. People think</span>
  <span id="freeText16135401283051110102" style="display:none"><b>Lothaire (Immortals after Dark, #12: 5 Star read that doesn't fail to deliver an amazing read</b><br /><br /><b>General Thoughts:</b> I love this series beyond reason. How is it that every freaking book manages to get better and better. I have no clue. Hopefully you are in the process of reading this book or reading the series because I can't help but feel like its one of the best ones out there. I never read paranormal romance until I stumbled across this series and it was the best stumble I've ever had. People think i'm so odd when i sit around squealing over a book about immortal beings , but you have to read it to understand! <br /><br /><br />Ok I finally have time to review and what better way to express my love of this book than with an Acronym! <br /><br /><i><b>L</b> othaire:</i> <br /><blockquote>He is just so sigh worthy. Unlike some people, I never had a problem with Lothaire. Yes, he popped up at the most horrid times and was an ass. However, I knew he was going to get his. I always knew that the one thing he couldn't defy was his immortal nature. When his bride came-a-callin' I figured he would get his just desserts. I really loved finding out who the true Lothaire was. In the end, he is nothing but a really sad product of his environment. Everything that concerned him was tainted with some sort of betrayal, torture, or evilness. I enjoyed his intelligence immensely and his struggle. He is just one of those characters I could honestly read about for a long time. I was always interested in what he was going to do or what he had done. He is so misunderstood. There is a part in the novel when he is talking to Nix and he simply states that he "feels old." He wanted Emily back because for once he felt young and alive. I love that moment. It was poignant and it was the moment When i fully empathized with Lothaire. Reminded me of when Nick Carraway in The Great Gatsby said <i>I'm 5 years to old to lie to myself and call it honor</i>...</blockquote><br /><br /><i><b>O</b> bcession</i> <br /><blockquote> Thats right. I'm freaking obsessed. I mean, I was already obsessed by the time I read this book. However, this one multiplied it by like a million. I'm just not a person who likes to read series for some reason but this series is my exception to everything<br /><br /><i><b>T</b> ragedy:</i><br /><blockquote>There was a hint of tragedy that surrounded everything in this novel. Lothaire's past. Emily's present circumstances...( i shall stay ambigious on that as to not spoil it :P) The state of the Lore. It added a seriousness to the novel. What I love about these novels is that every action effects something big in the Lore, whether we know what it is or not. The tragedy surrounding Lotharie and Emily cemented the importance of all their actions.</blockquote><br /><br /><i><b>H</b> eroine:</i><br /><blockquote>OMG. Emily was freaking amazing! Kresley Cole surprised the shit out of me with this girl. She was everything you just wouldn't expect in a mate for lothaire. The best part about her was that I compltely knew the type of girl she is. I'm from Indiana, home of corn and Nascar so I felt like I knew Emily personally. It is just hilarious that Mr. sophisticated vampire lotharie is matched to this girl from Appalachia! She was so strong. Her life was hell in a handbasket but she still endeavored to fight her circumstances. she always had an ace card. I liked her better than freaking Lothaire. She was too good for him to be honesty. Plus <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ any girl who sends her f***king middle finger to a man in response is my girl FOR LIFE! <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span></blockquote><br /><br /><i><b>A</b> ction:</i><br /><blockquote>There was a nice amount of action in this novel. I generally knew what was going to happen in the end, however, I could never predict HOW it was going to happen. It really made this novel fun to read as well as exciting ^_^ </blockquote><br /><br /><i><b>I</b> mprovement:</i><br /><blockquote> This series just keeps getting better. I know it sounds cliche but immortals after dark is very much so like wine. The world building is superb, the coupling, the actions, the plot, the suspense. Everything is so good. Each book gets better. I can hardly wait for the next one. I love seeing a writer improve with each book. It shows how much KC cares about her readers and her work.</blockquote> <br /><br /><i><b>R</b> epartee:</i><br /><blockquote>The freaking banter in this novel is like no other. I love LOVE a good snide remark. The sarcasm and wit was just endless in this novel. Lothaire is such a dick! The things he said were atrocious...I laughed out loud so much. He is just my type of guy bad mouthed and sarcastic. And lovely Emily gave it right back. She didn't take any shit! I loved it. KC can write banter like no other. I could read her quotes all day!!<br /><br /><i><b>E</b> roticism:</i><br /><blockquote> OMG OMG OMG! This book was EEEEEROTIC! I was reading this book in a class and it was damn near impossible to keep a straight face. My boyfriend kept asking me why i was blushing ( which is a feat since I have dark skin!). The sex was hot hot hot. I should know, I just got done re reading a scene for like the 100th time... hehe </blockquote><br /><br /><br />Well that ends my acronoym, i don't think i will be doing that again. It took forever. LOL<br /><br /><b>Points of Concern</b><br /><br />So this book/series did raise some things to my attention.<br /><br />1. Word on the street is KC is going to be doing a YA series...Idk how i feel about that. I do know I'm not excited... Its pretty obvious who it would star <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Thad probably <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> <br /><br />2. Blood and Mist Series<br /> I'm excited, however, I'm so invested in this lorean world already. There are so many coupling I've yet to see!! I hope those don't get put on the back burner<br /><br />3. Nix...I'm worried<br /><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ In this book, I really was faced with just how unhealthy nix is sounding. She is doing so freaking much for everyone. Not to mention, she is not very lucid. Lothaire was so right when she said she needed a man to come and help carry her burden. I'm all about independent woman but the girl has been holding the world together for freaking centuries. She needs a damn break. I would never forgive KC or this series if anything happened to her that was permanent! Nix deserves love more than ANYONE of those immortals :[ <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><br /></blockquote></blockquote></span>

He’s one of the meanest, cruelest, arrogant, controlling, sadistic, insulting, jealous, possessive, psychotic, bloody, black-clawed characters out there.   <span id="freeText10388769353706507295" style="display:none">Hello my friends. I’m here to pay tribute to one of the most important characters from the series <i>Immortals After Dark</i>. He’s one of the meanest, cruelest, arrogant, controlling, sadistic, insulting, jealous, possessive, psychotic, bloody, black-clawed characters out there. Let’s hear it for the one, the only, the Enemy of Old, Lothaire!<br><br>*Tchaikovsky’s <i><a href="http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=C0MuG6Ca16o" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"></a>”Dance of the Mirlitons”</i> playing in the background*<br> <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380348854ra/702979.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br> <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380348854ra/702980.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br> <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380348854ra/702981.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br> <br><span>[image error]</span><br> <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380348854ra/702983.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br> <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380348854i/702984.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Yes Lothaire. I’ve depleted all my wall-punching gifs for you. Because you’re worth it!<br><br>Seriously now, being in a relationship with this dude would be a nightmare. But I have to admit he’s fun as hell. He and I share some similar opinions on life and people.<br><blockquote>
  <i> “When mortals ask me incessant questions, I customarily snatch out their tongues and watch them bleed to death.”<br><br>“I often help others discover the outer limits of their hatred. It’s a talent of mine.”<br><br>Apparently, he’d killed so many family members that he must have significantly affected the Lore’s population. Doing my part for the environment.</i>
</blockquote><br>How can’t you admire a person like him? You actually can’t at times. The bastard got me so angry I could punch a wall. Oh wait.<br> <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380348854ra/702985.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>*ouch*<br><br>Anyway, <i>Lothaire</i> was loads of fun! <div id="review_386023576" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/386023576" />
    <a title="Val ⚓️ Shameless Non-Snowflake ⚓️" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11626803-val-shameless-non-snowflake"><img alt="Val ⚓️ Shameless Non-Snowflake ⚓️" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1605987751p2/11626803.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/386023576?book_show_action=true">Aug 07, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Val ⚓️ Shameless Non-Snowflake ⚓️" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Val ⚓️ Shameless Non-Snowflake ⚓️" href="/user/show/11626803-val-shameless-non-snowflake">Val ⚓️ Shameless Non-Snowflake ⚓️</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11626803-val-shameless-non-snowflake?shelf=paranormal">paranormal</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11626803-val-shameless-non-snowflake?shelf=age-gap">age-gap</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11626803-val-shameless-non-snowflake?shelf=vampires">vampires</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11626803-val-shameless-non-snowflake?shelf=1-stars">1-stars</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
                  <em>
                    This review has been hidden because it contains spoilers. To view it,
                    <a href="#" onclick="Effect.toggle(&#39;reviewTextContainer386023576&#39;); return false;">click here.</a>
                  </em>
              <span id="reviewTextContainer386023576" class="readable"
                    style="display:none"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12808262601808611913">I am BAFFLED by all the good reviews. I have read this entire series and was eagerly anticipating this book. What a disappointment. Usually I stay up all night in order to finish books from this series because I literally can't put them down, but I actually had to force myself to even finish this book at all.<br/><br/>First of all, I understand that Lothaire is not a "good guy." That has been established in the previous books; however, I feel like his behavior could have been spun differently so as to mak</span>
  <span id="freeText12808262601808611913" style="display:none">I am BAFFLED by all the good reviews. I have read this entire series and was eagerly anticipating this book. What a disappointment. Usually I stay up all night in order to finish books from this series because I literally can't put them down, but I actually had to force myself to even finish this book at all.<br /><br />First of all, I understand that Lothaire is not a "good guy." That has been established in the previous books; however, I feel like his behavior could have been spun differently so as to make him at least likeable in this book, which Cole just did not do. She tried to set up a background for Lothaire to explain why he is the way he is (which I won't go into here), but it just fell short for me. Also, if I had to read the words "end game" one more time I probably would have thrown the book across the room.<br /><br />I thought the whole premise of Ellie being possessed by Lothaire's potential vampire bride, Saroya, was brilliant. And it started off really well. Somewhere along the way, however, (perhaps midway through) Cole seemed to lose steam. The story just wasn't going anywhere and the constant discussion about doing something to get the ring from La Dorada and subsequently banishing Ellie's soul just became redundant. It was almost like, enough already, stop talking about it and do it or shut up.<br /><br />Also, SPOILER ALERT, I understand that Lothaire is an uber alpha male and all that, which I usually love. But when he turns Ellie into a vampire against her will, in the face of her flagrant and vehemently stated objections, I was annoyed. And when he didn't even apologize, flying the "I know what's best for you" flag, I was even more annoyed. BUT when Ellie, who up until that point was pretty strong and independent, just kind of accepted that without a fight, I was just over the book.<br /><br />I felt like there was a lot of build up around the premise of Lothaire realizing and accepting mortal Ellie as his bride, but when it actually happened it was pretty anticlimactic. And he didn't really accept her as a mortal. I felt like he didn't accept her until he turned her (against her will) and made her into an immortal, which to me doesn't scream true and unconditional love. Long story short, it almost seemed like Cole just said forget it and wanted to finish the book. </span>
  <a data-text-id="12808262601808611913" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer163230770" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2188034094874487725"><br/><b>5 Brilliant Stars for the delicious Lothaire! No one writes paranormal romance like Kresley Cole...she is #1 in my book!!</b><br/><br/>Picture Eric Northman from True Blood dating Ellie Mae Clampett from the Beverly Hillbillies, and you have <i>Lothaire</i>!! <br/><br/>The pairing of Lothaire and Elizabeth was nothing short of brilliant. My initial hope was that Nix was meant for Lothaire, being that they are the two oldest creatures that still exist in the world of The Lore. My thinking can’t hold a candle to the wisdom and </span>
  <span id="freeText2188034094874487725" style="display:none"><br /><b>5 Brilliant Stars for the delicious Lothaire! No one writes paranormal romance like Kresley Cole...she is #1 in my book!!</b><br /><br />Picture Eric Northman from True Blood dating Ellie Mae Clampett from the Beverly Hillbillies, and you have <i>Lothaire</i>!! <br /><br />The pairing of Lothaire and Elizabeth was nothing short of brilliant. My initial hope was that Nix was meant for Lothaire, being that they are the two oldest creatures that still exist in the world of The Lore. My thinking can’t hold a candle to the wisdom and brilliance of Kelsey Cole, because she wrote another extraordinary installment in this amazing series.<br /> <br />Now that Lothaire’s heart beats again and his blood flows, it’s been heading south and his 'soldier' stands at the ready, as it springs back to life. *snort* He is one sexy voracious vampire!<b>RAWRRRRR!!</b> He has much to teach Elizabeth, but she’s not sure that he’s the one for her. The off the cuff banter between Lothaire and Elizabeth was sharp, funny, and had me laughing throughout the book. Whether in the heat of the moment or in a heated argument, they were fantastic together. Along for the ride were many of our favorite characters from the previous books, and a few new ones. The sweet Thaddeus befriends Elizabeth, along with Balery the Hag, Lothiare’s oracle. When the three of them hang out, it’s like college buddies reuniting. Nucking Futs Nix is back with her predictions and insight, and she’s crazier than ever. Lothiare and Nix have a brief respite from fighting; they let down their guard and reminisce. It was very sweet and sort of sad. <br /><br />The ending was surprising and has me anxious for the next book. As the series gears towards a conclusion and the Accession nears, you can’t help but wonder who will be together in the end. Is there someone special for our favorite Valkyrie, Nix?? I have yet to be disappointed in this fabulous series and I’m quite sure Kresley Cole will work her magic once again. <br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="2188034094874487725" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_154625074" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/154625074" />
    <a title="Laura" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2043222-laura"><img alt="Laura" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1577660807p2/2043222.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/154625074?book_show_action=true">Mar 15, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Laura" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Laura" href="/user/show/2043222-laura">Laura</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer154625074" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5281546172769802438"><br/><br/><a href='http://www.gotfiction.com/lothaire-by-kresley-cole/' rel='nofollow noopener'>review posted on Got Fiction? book blog</a><br/><br/>The beginning of this book sucks you in, it traps you, and it doesn’t let you go. By the time you finish, you realize the whole day has passed, and you haven’t fed your children or husband, or even grabbed a coffee. Just me? I didn’t think so.<br/><br/>I wasn’t sure how much I’d like Lothaire as a hero, I mean he has had his moments, but always with a price. We find out why he’s been hoarding these “favors” owed to him. And we find out just how much he’s willing to g</span>
  <span id="freeText5281546172769802438" style="display:none"><br /><br /><a href="http://www.gotfiction.com/lothaire-by-kresley-cole/" rel="nofollow noopener">review posted on Got Fiction? book blog</a><br /><br />The beginning of this book sucks you in, it traps you, and it doesn’t let you go. By the time you finish, you realize the whole day has passed, and you haven’t fed your children or husband, or even grabbed a coffee. Just me? I didn’t think so.<br /><br />I wasn’t sure how much I’d like Lothaire as a hero, I mean he has had his moments, but always with a price. We find out why he’s been hoarding these “favors” owed to him. And we find out just how much he’s willing to give up for those favors, if anything.<br /><br />Ellie is the complete antithesis of Lothaire. She’s a mountain girl through and through, but she’s possessed by a demon, so she thinks. Around age 18, she starts having blackouts and waking up to carnage, blood, and heaps of questions. After dealing with the murders, she decides to go out fighting. Suicide by cop. She grabs a shotgun, steps out in front of the police, and is instantly protected by Lothaire. Who is seriously pissed, by the way. So he tells her that she will go to prison where she can be safe from herself an others, until he can come for her. Surprise surprise, Lothaire found his bride. But it’s not Ellie, it can’t be this uncouth, barefoot mountain girl. It is of course, the vampire goddess inside of her. So off to death row for 19 year old Ellie, until Lothaire can find a way to separate her soul from Saroya, his vampire goddess bride.<br /><br />5 years later, Ellie is strapped to the table, waiting for her death sentence by lethal injection, and who shows up once more? Lothaire, of course. Taking her with him, he decides he’ll keep her hostage until he can retrieve the Ring of Sums and he’ll use that to separate Ellie from her body. But he sort of realizes that Ellie may be his bride after all, not the frigid vampire goddess Saroya.<br /><br />Oops, did Lothaire send his Bride to Death Row? And oops, has he treated her like crap? And oh, was he just as high-handed as they come? I think Kresley Cole has an amazing talent of having her heroes do things that I hate, behave in ways I hate, and yet I still like the hero. She gets me every time. <br /><br />I loved how Ellie not only could hold her own with him, but she made him like her. <i>Her</i>, not Saroya. And the best part? Ellie made him question his <b>End Game.</b><br /><br />My fave quote has a teeny bit of spoiler for scene set up:<br /><br />After a huge fight between them, Ellie is kidnapped by the Valkyries to be used as leverage against Lothaire. He sends her his heart, in a gift wrapped box with a note telling her, she had his heart, it’s the only one she’ll ever get from him. (I won’t spoil what she send him back, but it gives her street cred with the Valkyries, it’s just that awesome). So when they finally get back together, Ellie asks him if he didn’t want her, after all, he’d sent her his heart. He offers her, claws to his chest, his new heart muttering, <br /><br /><i>“Take this one, My heart doesn't fucking working right without you.”</i><br /><br />Best scene in the book. Best line ever. I forgave him his alphahole tendencies then and there. This intense hero, mad as a hatter, made me love him from the first page. I loved his relationship with Ellie, and I loved watching him fall for Ellie, even when he was an ass to her. Ellie is one of my favorite heroines yet--I just adored her. <br /><br />The only thing I didn’t like, is that I wish that he’d understood [certain things I can't spoil] without having to dream her memories, I mean I get why, but still, would have been nice to see him understand without that. But I am just dying to see what happens with Kristoff, Fury, Cara, Nix, and all of the characters who we love. Kresley Cole has reminded me of why she is one of my favorite authors ever.<br /><br />***Thank you to Simon &amp; Schuster for the the book</span>
  <a data-text-id="5281546172769802438" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_159739256" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/159739256" />
    <a title="valee" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2320890-valee"><img alt="valee" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1443365004p2/2320890.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/159739256?book_show_action=true">Apr 08, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="valee" class="user" itemprop="url" name="valee" href="/user/show/2320890-valee">valee</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Hardcover 9780857207975" href="/book/show/13112924-lothaire">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2320890-valee?shelf=amazing-pnr-romance">amazing-pnr-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer159739256" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12286346480044623837"><blockquote>“Admit it, love, you like it when I'm a little bad....” </blockquote><br/><b>Shit, this book just didn't allow me to go out with my friends </b>(even though it's friday night and I have been craving for a little free time since monday) <b>nor do ANYTHING else, for a matter of fact. I just COULDN'T PUT IT DOWN!</b> It has been ages since I was THIS fixated with a book. I can't even remember the last time I added a book to my favs list. I always adored this series and I definitely can say it is one of the best in the paranormal-</span>
  <span id="freeText12286346480044623837" style="display:none"><blockquote>“Admit it, love, you like it when I'm a little bad....” </blockquote><br /><b>Shit, this book just didn't allow me to go out with my friends </b>(even though it's friday night and I have been craving for a little free time since monday) <b>nor do ANYTHING else, for a matter of fact. I just COULDN'T PUT IT DOWN!</b> It has been ages since I was THIS fixated with a book. I can't even remember the last time I added a book to my favs list. I always adored this series and I definitely can say it is one of the best in the paranormal-romance genre. But more than that, I'm glad to say this book is just as good as the others if not better.<br /><br /><b>Lothaire was definitely one of those heroes you don't know if to love or to hate. </b>He has always been the 'bad guy' but once we get to know him better we can understand why he is the way he is and did the things he did. I always believe people are the way they are for a reason so to get to know those reasons always makes me feel closer to the characters. I adored Lothaire, although I thought he would be a much complicated and complex hero. He is pretty easy to understand once you get to know him. The heroine was good for him, she just knew exactly which of his buttons to push. <br /><br /><b>But I know that the reason for why I adore the books in this series so much is because of the author </b>and not the characters. While I enjoy reading about all the characters of this series, it's the way everything is so amazingly well-described and this outstanding new and perplexing world what I love the most. I know she could keep writing more books and I just would keep reading them because there is no one thing I adore about this series. There's just something too appealing about this series that doesn't let me wait long to put my hands on a new book for long. <br /><br />And I just can't help adoring how I always laugh and laugh with them! Those Valks will always be some of the best characters I have EVER read about.<br /><blockquote><br />“As Lothaire lifted the lid with a sense of dread, Nïx murmured, “Hint: it’s the middle one.” <br />Elizabeth’s fragile finger.Seeing it severed like this brought on a visceral reaction—pain shooting through his own hand, radiating throughout his regenerated heart. He closed the lid with a swallow, sentimentally pocketing the package. <br />“You gave her your heart, and she gave you the bird.” Nïx sighed. “Songs will be written about this.” </blockquote></span>
  <a data-text-id="12286346480044623837" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1103486792" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1103486792" />
    <a title="Carmel (Rabid Reads)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4561998-carmel-rabid-reads"><img alt="Carmel (Rabid Reads)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1396922701p2/4561998.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1103486792?book_show_action=true">Nov 11, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Carmel (Rabid Reads)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Carmel (Rabid Reads)" href="/user/show/4561998-carmel-rabid-reads">Carmel (Rabid Reads)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Audible Audio " href="/book/show/13410709-lothaire">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4561998-carmel-rabid-reads?shelf=audio">audio</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4561998-carmel-rabid-reads?shelf=audio-2015">audio-2015</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1103486792" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2826343225324822194"><b>Reviewed by: <a href='http://rabidreads.ca/2015/11/audiobook-review-lothaire-by-kresley-cole-kresleycole-petkoff-simonaudio.html' rel='nofollow noopener'>Rabid Reads</a></b>.<br/><br/>The hype vis-à-vis LOTHAIRE’s story has been gradually building with every IMMORTALS AFTER DARK installment, and albeit three years later, I now understand why all of my fellow bloggers were fan-girling it up over the Enemy of Old. Most authors hold back when developing their anti-heroes because there’s a thin line between Bad Boy and a-hole, but not Kresley Cole, she went full-on bastard, and I absolutely loved her for it!<br/><br/>Every addition to this series brings with it its</span>
  <span id="freeText2826343225324822194" style="display:none"><b>Reviewed by: <a href="http://rabidreads.ca/2015/11/audiobook-review-lothaire-by-kresley-cole-kresleycole-petkoff-simonaudio.html" rel="nofollow noopener">Rabid Reads</a></b>.<br /><br />The hype vis-à-vis LOTHAIRE’s story has been gradually building with every IMMORTALS AFTER DARK installment, and albeit three years later, I now understand why all of my fellow bloggers were fan-girling it up over the Enemy of Old. Most authors hold back when developing their anti-heroes because there’s a thin line between Bad Boy and a-hole, but not Kresley Cole, she went full-on bastard, and I absolutely loved her for it!<br /><br />Every addition to this series brings with it its own romantic flavour, and none of them have been repeats which after eleven novels is gosh darned impressive. The plot threads of all that has come before continue to intermingle in startling ways, and characters reach new levels of growth even though their tale has already been, or has yet to be told. The century long feud between the Black King and the White Queen left me chomping at the bit for more, and I hope that Thad gets his own title because well, listen to a sound clip, and you’ll get it.<br /><br />I liked that Cole dedicated several chapters to fleshing out Lothaire’s history; it painted a clear picture of his depravity, and the unbreakable vows that bind him. Daciano is Evil with a capital E, and I don’t in any way approve of his treatment of Ellie, but when cruelty has always been a part of your life, happiness seems like a pipe dream. It’s funny how the mate you want, and the one you need can be two worlds apart; Elizabeth’s stubbornness, trailer park ways, and blood is thicker than water views on family made her the perfect for Leo.<br /><br />The narrator’s mountain twang demonstrated for the umpteenth time that even the most far-out POV is akin to child’s play when left in his capable hands. Robert Petkoff’s transitions between Russian immortal royalty, and Appalachian hillbilly had me sweating bullets one moment, and hollering with redneck sisterhood the next. The voice he used for La Dorada still keeps me up at night sometimes while as Thaddeus’ Texan accent has scored prime real estate in my audiobook spank bank. Oops, did I just say that about a seventeen year old albeit fictional man? How embarrassing.<br /><br />Come over to the dark side… We have cookies and LOTHAIRE.</span>
  <a data-text-id="2826343225324822194" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('RjtmmVSYZkqoIaodsaaV4SLu+HNndlgOZAYY73Zsdx2OIjmYgy4m5qcboQtK/wXYIotIm3z5HKf/Xthp3xVvUQ==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('Z9q0SrAdPLGs2PQDs7WZYu+lJrUWDscxgBD6qaml872vw+tLZ6t8HaPi/xVI7Alb78CWXQ2Bg5gbSDovANzr8Q==')})
  }
//]]>

<span id="freeTextContainer11802239738772415819">Kresley Cole is the #1 <i>New York Times</i> bestselling author of the electrifying Immortals After Dark paranormal series, the young adult Arcana Chronicles series, the erotic Gamemakers series, and five award-winning historical romances.<br/><br/>A master’s grad and former athlete, she has traveled over much of the world and draws from those experiences to create her memorable characters and settings. <br/>Her IAD bo</span>
  <span id="freeText11802239738772415819" style="display:none">Kresley Cole is the #1 <i>New York Times</i> bestselling author of the electrifying Immortals After Dark paranormal series, the young adult Arcana Chronicles series, the erotic Gamemakers series, and five award-winning historical romances.<br /><br />A master’s grad and former athlete, she has traveled over much of the world and draws from those experiences to create her memorable characters and settings. <br />Her IAD books have been translated into 23 foreign languages, garnered three RITA awards, a RWA Hall of Fame induction, and consistently appear on the bestseller lists, in the U.S. and abroad.<br /><br />Cole lives in Florida with her family. Learn more about Kresley at: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.kresleycole.com">www.kresleycole.com</a> &amp; <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.thearcanachronicles.com">www.thearcanachronicles.com</a><br /><br /></span>
